1.5; max-width: 200px; text-align: center;"><span class="nodeLabel"><p>shareVin directly</p></span></div></foreignObject></g></g></g></g></g></svg>

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant ShareModal
    participant Redux
    participant API
    
    User->>ShareModal: Opens modal (show=true)
    ShareModal->>Redux: clearShareVin(true)
    User->>ShareModal: Enters email addresses
    ShareModal->>ShareModal: Validates emails with isValidEmail
    User->>ShareModal: Adjusts map (if HereMapPlatform)
    User->>ShareModal: Clicks Share button
    
    alt HereMapPlatform
        ShareModal->>Redux: setShouldCaptureScreenshot(true)
        Redux->>ShareModal: capturedScreenshot updated
        ShareModal->>API: shareVin(emails, screenshot, timezone)
    else Other Platform
        ShareModal->>API: shareVin(emails, null, timezone)
    end
    
    alt Success
        API->>Redux: isShareVinSuccessful = true
        Redux->>ShareModal: Update props
        ShareModal->>Redux: clearShareVin(false)
        ShareModal->>Redux: setCapturedScreenshot(null)
        ShareModal->>ShareModal: Reset email input
        ShareModal->>User: Show success alert
    else Failure
        API->>Redux: isShareVinFailed = true
        Redux->>ShareModal: Update props
        ShareModal->>User: Show error alert
    end
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class ShareModal {
        +show: bool
        +hide: func
        +mapPlatform: string
        +clearShareVin: func
        +shareVin: func
        +isSharingVin: bool
        +isShareVinSuccessful: bool
        +isShareVinFailed: bool
        +setShouldCaptureScreenshot: func
        +shouldCaptureScreenshot: bool
        +capturedScreenshot: string
        +setCapturedScreenshot: func
        +canShareEta: bool
        -emails: state
        -hasValidEmails: computed
        -timezone: computed
        -descriptionLabel: computed
        +render() Modal
    }
    
    class Modal {
        +backdrop: string
        +show: bool
        +onHide: func
    }
    
    class ModalHeader {
        +closeButton: bool
        +css: object
        +title: string
    }
    
    class ModalBody {
        +css: object
        +children: ReactNode
    }
    
    class ModalFooter {
        +style: object
        +children: ReactNode
    }
    
    class RoutingMap {
        +allowCaptureScreenshot: bool
        +showHeatmap: bool
    }
    
    class Redux {
        +mapStateToProps()
        +mapDispatchToProps()
    }
    
    ShareModal --> Modal
    Modal --> ModalHeader
    Modal --> ModalBody
    Modal --> ModalFooter
    ModalBody --> RoutingMap
    ShareModal --> Redux
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> ModalClosed
    ModalClosed --> ModalOpen: show=true
    ModalOpen --> EmailEntry: User types
    EmailEntry --> EmailEntry: Validation check
    EmailEntry --> MapAdjustment: HereMapPlatform only
    MapAdjustment --> ReadyToShare: hasValidEmails
    EmailEntry --> ReadyToShare: hasValidEmails & !HereMapPlatform
    ReadyToShare --> Capturing: Click Share & HereMapPlatform
    Capturing --> Sharing: Screenshot captured
    ReadyToShare --> Sharing: Click Share & !HereMapPlatform
    Sharing --> Success: shareVin succeeds
    Sharing --> Failed: shareVin fails
    Success --> ModalOpen: Show success alert
    Failed --> ModalOpen: Show error alert
    ModalOpen --> ModalClosed: Click Close
    Success --> ModalClosed: Auto-reset after success
```
